# [cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks

**Repository:** pytorch  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix



## Description

cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on version checks but currently only the compile-time version is exposed. To allow users to resolve cuDNN version mismatches by updating their cuDNN installation locally, the runtime version needs to be checked rather than the compile-time version.

## Task

Expose the cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks so that dispatching heuristics (SDPA, Convolution) can use it instead of the compile-time version.

Description: cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on version checks but currently only the compile-time version is exposed. The runtime version needs to be checked so that users who update their cuDNN installation locally get correct dispatching behavior.

Changes:
- 7 files modified
- 43 additions, 9 deletions

Tasks:
1. Find where cuDNN version checks are done in CUDA hooks and dispatching code
2. Add runtime version retrieval and expose it alongside the compile-time version
3. Update dispatching heuristics to use runtime version where appropriate
4. Verify your changes compile and match the expected fix

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 7 modified files updated correctly.

## Testing

Your implementation will be automatically verified:

```
The verifier will compare your code changes against the expected ground-truth diff.
Score = 0.35 * file_recall + 0.45 * line_recall + 0.20 * line_precision
```

802026-03-11T18:18:31.241160agentmessage-
All four changes are correct and complete. Here's a summary of what was done and why:

---

## Changes Made

### 1. `aten/src/ATen/native/ConvUtils.h` (1 line changed)
`cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format()` used `versionCuDNN()` (compile-time `CUDNN_VERSION`) to decide whether to suggest `ChannelsLast` / `ChannelsLast3d` memory formats. Changed to `versionRuntimeCuDNN()` so the heuristic reflects the actually-linked cuDNN library instead of the one PyTorch was compiled against.

### 2. `aten/src/ATen/native/transformers/cuda/sdp_utils.cpp` (1 line removed, 4 lines added)
`check_prefer_cudnn_attention()` was gated by a compile-time preprocessor check `#if (defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && (CUDNN_VERSION >= 90900))`. Replaced with an `#if AT_CUDNN_ENABLED()` guard and a runtime check `versionRuntimeCuDNN() >= 90900`, using a `static` local so the version is fetched only once. This means the SDPA backend priority order (cudnn-first on SM90/SM100) now activates correctly when the user upgrades their cuDNN at runtime, even if PyTorch was built against an older version.

### 3. `aten/src/ATen/cudnn/Types.h` (1 line added)
Declared `cudnn_runtime_version()` alongside the existing compile-time `cudnn_version()`, giving cuDNN-aware code (files that `#include <ATen/cudnn/Types.h>`) a clean accessor for the runtime version.

### 4. `aten/src/ATen/cudnn/Types.cpp` (4 lines added)
Implemented `cudnn_runtime_version()` by delegating to `at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN()`. The include chain `<ATen/ATen.h>` → `<ATen/Context.h>` → `<ATen/detail/CUDAHooksInterface.h>` already provides `getCUDAHooks()`, so no new includes were needed.

I am thinking...: The remaining compile-time check at line 668 is:
```cpp
#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && CUDNN_VERSION < 90000
  if (debug) {
    TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, " cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)");
  }
  return false;
#endif
```

This is a compile-time guard that says "if compiled with cuDNN < 9.0.0, then can_use_cudnn_attention always returns false."

Should this be changed to a runtime check?

The check at line 668 says "CUDNN_VERSION < 90000" - this is checking if the COMPILE-TIME version is older than 9.0. If we're running with a newer cuDNN at runtime, this would still return false even though the runtime library supports it.

However, looking at the context more carefully - there's also the WARN message that says `CUDNN_VERSION` (the compile-time version). And the function has the outer check at line 662 that already handles "not built with cuDNN."

For the `can_use_cudnn_attention` function, this check is particularly tricky because:
1. The line 662 guard `#if defined(USE_ROCM) || !AT_CUDNN_ENABLED() || !defined(CUDNN_VERSION)` - if CUDNN_VERSION is not defined, we return false already
2. The line 668 guard `#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && CUDNN_VERSION < 90000` - if compile-time version < 9.0.0, return false

Now, the PR is about using runtime version. Should this `CUDNN_VERSION < 90000` check also be converted to runtime? It depends on whether this is a "dispatch heuristic" or a "feature gate."

For `check_prefer_cudnn_attention()` (the one I already changed at line 83), it was using compile-time version to decide whether to prefer cuDNN SDPA. That's a dispatch heuristic.

For `can_use_cudnn_attention()`, the `CUDNN_VERSION < 90000` check is a "feature gate" - it says cuDNN attention doesn't even EXIST before 9.0.0. Even if you h

Here's a complete summary:\n\n## Changes Applied\n\n### 1. `aten/src/ATen/native/ConvUtils.h`\n**`cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format()`** \u2014 swapped compile-time `versionCuDNN()` (returns `CUDNN_VERSION` macro) for `versionRuntimeCuDNN()` (calls `cudnnGetVersion()`). This means the ChannelsLast/ChannelsLast3d memory format eligibility thresholds (7603, 8005) are now checked against the actually-loaded cuDNN library, not the one PyTorch was built with.\n\n### 2. `aten/src/ATen/native/transformers/cuda/sdp_utils.cpp`\n**`check_prefer_cudnn_attention()`** \u2014 replaced the preprocessor gate `#if (defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && (CUDNN_VERSION >= 90900))` with an `#if AT_CUDNN_ENABLED()` guard plus a runtime check:\n```cpp\nstatic long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\nif (cudnn_version < 90900) { return false; }\n```\nThe `static` local ensures a single call per process lifetime. Previously, upgrading cuDNN from 8.x to 9.9+ at runtime (without recompiling PyTorch) could never activate the cuDNN-first SDPA priority order.\n\n### 3. `aten/src/ATen/cudnn/Types.h` + `Types.cpp`\nAdded `cudnn_runtime_version()` alongside the existing compile-time `cudnn_version()`:\n- **Header**: `int64_t cudnn_runtime_version();`\n- **Implementation**: `return at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();`\n\nThis gives any cuDNN-aware code that `#include`s `Types.h` a clean, hook-dispatched accessor for the runtime version, symmetrically matching the existing `cudnn_version()` compile-time accessor.\n\n### Pre-existing (already correct in repo)\nThe hook infrastructure (`CUDAHooksInterface.h`, `CUDAHooks.h`, `CUDAHooks.cpp`), `Context.h` wrapper, `Convolution.cpp` (lines 416, 460), other `sdp_utils.cpp` runtime calls (lines 444, 675), and `torch/csrc/cuda/shared/cudnn.cpp::getVersionInt()` were already using `versionRuntimeCuDNN()` and required no further changes.\n\nThe one remaining `#if CUDNN_VERSION < 90000` in `can_use_cudnn_attention()` is intentionally left as a compile-time gate \u2014 it guards against calling 9.x attention APIs that were never compiled into the binary, not a runtime dispatch decision."
